     1	// Copyright 2018 The Hugo Authors. All rights reserved.

    10	// WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
    11	// See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
    12	// limitations under the License.
    13	
    14	// Package minifiers contains minifiers mapped to MIME types. This package is used
    15	// in both the resource transformation, i.e. resources.Minify, and in the publishing
    16	// chain.
    17	package minifiers
    18	
    19	import (
    20	        "io"
    21	        "regexp"
    22	
    23	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/config"
    24	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/output"
    25	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/transform"
    26	
    27	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/media"
    28	        "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2"
    29	)
    30	
    31	// Client wraps a minifier.
    32	type Client struct {
    33	        // Whether output minification is enabled (HTML in /public)
    34	        MinifyOutput bool
    35	
    36	        m *minify.M
    37	}
    38	
    39	// Transformer returns a func that can be used in the transformer publishing chain.
    40	// TODO(bep) minify config etc
    41	func (m Client) Transformer(mediatype media.Type) transform.Transformer {
    42	        _, params, min := m.m.Match(mediatype.Type)
    43	        if min == nil {
    44	                // No minifier for this MIME type
    45	                return nil
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        return func(ft transform.FromTo) error {
    49	                // Note that the source io.Reader will already be buffered, but it implements
    50	                // the Bytes() method, which is recognized by the Minify library.
    51	                return min.Minify(m.m, ft.To(), ft.From(), params)
    52	        }
    53	}
    54	
    55	// Minify tries to minify the src into dst given a MIME type.
    56	func (m Client) Minify(mediatype media.Type, dst io.Writer, src io.Reader) error {
    57	        return m.m.Minify(mediatype.Type, dst, src)
    58	}
    59	
    60	// noopMinifier implements minify.Minifier [1], but doesn't minify content. This means
    61	// that we can avoid missing minifiers for any MIME types in our minify.M, which
    62	// causes minify to return errors, while still allowing minification to be
    63	// disabled for specific types.
    64	//
    65	// [1]: https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/tdewolff/minify#Minifier
    66	type noopMinifier struct{}
    67	
    68	// Minify copies r into w without transformation.
    69	func (m noopMinifier) Minify(_ *minify.M, w io.Writer, r io.Reader, _ map[string]string) error {
    70	        _, err := io.Copy(w, r)
    71	        return err
    72	}
    73	
    74	// New creates a new Client with the provided MIME types as the mapping foundation.
    75	// The HTML minifier is also registered for additional HTML types (AMP etc.) in the
    76	// provided list of output formats.
    77	func New(mediaTypes media.Types, outputFormats output.Formats, cfg config.AllProvider) (Client, error) {
    78	        conf := cfg.GetConfigSection("minify").(MinifyConfig)
    79	        m := minify.New()
    80	
    81	        // We use the Type definition of the media types defined in the site if found.
    82	        addMinifier(m, mediaTypes, "css", getMinifier(conf, "css"))
    83	
    84	        addMinifier(m, mediaTypes, "js", getMinifier(conf, "js"))
    85	        m.AddRegexp(regexp.MustCompile("^(application|text)/(x-)?(java|ecma)script$"), getMinifier(conf, "js"))
    86	
    87	        addMinifier(m, mediaTypes, "json", getMinifier(conf, "json"))
    88	        m.AddRegexp(regexp.MustCompile(`^(application|text)/(x-|(ld|manifest)\+)?json$`), getMinifier(conf, "json"))
    89	
    90	        addMinifier(m, mediaTypes, "svg", getMinifier(conf, "svg"))
    91	
    92	        addMinifier(m, mediaTypes, "xml", getMinifier(conf, "xml"))
    93	
    94	        // HTML
    95	        addMinifier(m, mediaTypes, "html", getMinifier(conf, "html"))
    96	        for _, of := range outputFormats {
    97	                if of.IsHTML {
    98	                        m.Add(of.MediaType.Type, getMinifier(conf, "html"))
    99	                }
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        return Client{m: m, MinifyOutput: conf.MinifyOutput}, nil
   103	}
   104	
   105	// getMinifier returns the appropriate minify.MinifierFunc for the MIME
   106	// type suffix s, given the config c.
   107	func getMinifier(c MinifyConfig, s string) minify.Minifier {
   108	        switch {
   109	        case s == "css" && !c.DisableCSS:
   110	                return &c.Tdewolff.CSS
   111	        case s == "js" && !c.DisableJS:
   112	                return &c.Tdewolff.JS
   113	        case s == "json" && !c.DisableJSON:
   114	                return &c.Tdewolff.JSON
   115	        case s == "svg" && !c.DisableSVG:
   116	                return &c.Tdewolff.SVG
   117	        case s == "xml" && !c.DisableXML:
   118	                return &c.Tdewolff.XML
   119	        case s == "html" && !c.DisableHTML:
   120	                return &c.Tdewolff.HTML
   121	        default:
   122	                return noopMinifier{}
   123	        }
   124	}
   125	
   126	func addMinifier(m *minify.M, mt media.Types, suffix string, min minify.Minifier) {
   127	        types := mt.BySuffix(suffix)
   128	        for _, t := range types {
   129	                m.Add(t.Type, min)
   130	        }
   131	}
   132

    14	package minifiers_test

    16	import (

    19	        "strings"

    21	
    22	        qt "github.com/frankban/quicktest"
    23	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/config"
    24	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/config/testconfig"
    25	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/media"

    31	func TestNew(t *testing.T) {
    32	        c := qt.New(t)
    33	        m, _ := minifiers.New(media.DefaultTypes, output.DefaultFormats, testconfig.GetTestConfig(afero.NewMemMapFs(), nil))
    34	
    35	        var rawJS string
    36	        var minJS string
    37	        rawJS = " var  foo =1 ;   foo ++  ;  "
    38	        minJS = "var foo=1;foo++"
    39	
    40	        var rawJSON string
    41	        var minJSON string
    42	        rawJSON = "  { \"a\" : 123 , \"b\":2,  \"c\": 5 } "
    43	        minJSON = "{\"a\":123,\"b\":2,\"c\":5}"
    44	
    45	        for _, test := range []struct {
    46	                tp                media.Type
    47	                rawString         string
    48	                expectedMinString string
    49	        }{
    50	                {media.Builtin.CSSType, " body { color: blue; }  ", "body{color:blue}"},
    51	                {media.Builtin.RSSType, " <hello>  Hugo!   </hello>  ", "<hello>Hugo!</hello>"}, // RSS should be handled as XML
    52	                {media.Builtin.JSONType, rawJSON, minJSON},
    53	                {media.Builtin.JavascriptType, rawJS, minJS},
    54	                // JS Regex minifiers
    55	                {media.Type{Type: "application/ecmascript", MainType: "application", SubType: "ecmascript"}, rawJS, minJS},
    56	                {media.Type{Type: "application/javascript", MainType: "application", SubType: "javascript"}, rawJS, minJS},
    57	                {media.Type{Type: "application/x-javascript", MainType: "application", SubType: "x-javascript"}, rawJS, minJS},
    58	                {media.Type{Type: "application/x-ecmascript", MainType: "application", SubType: "x-ecmascript"}, rawJS, minJS},
    59	                {media.Type{Type: "text/ecmascript", MainType: "text", SubType: "ecmascript"}, rawJS, minJS},
    60	                {media.Type{Type: "application/javascript", MainType: "text", SubType: "javascript"}, rawJS, minJS},
    61	                // JSON Regex minifiers
    62	                {media.Type{Type: "application/json", MainType: "application", SubType: "json"}, rawJSON, minJSON},
    63	                {media.Type{Type: "application/x-json", MainType: "application", SubType: "x-json"}, rawJSON, minJSON},
    64	                {media.Type{Type: "application/ld+json", MainType: "application", SubType: "ld+json"}, rawJSON, minJSON},
    65	                {media.Type{Type: "application/json", MainType: "text", SubType: "json"}, rawJSON, minJSON},
    66	        } {
    67	                var b bytes.Buffer
    68	
    69	                c.Assert(m.Minify(test.tp, &b, strings.NewReader(test.rawString)), qt.IsNil)
    70	                c.Assert(b.String(), qt.Equals, test.expectedMinString)
    71	        }
    72	}
    73	
    74	func TestConfigureMinify(t *testing.T) {
    75	        c := qt.New(t)
    76	        v := config.New()
    77	        v.Set("minify", map[string]any{
    78	                "disablexml": true,
    79	                "tdewolff": map[string]any{
    80	                        "html": map[string]any{
    81	                                "keepwhitespace": true,
    82	                        },
    83	                },
    84	        })
    85	        m, _ := minifiers.New(media.DefaultTypes, output.DefaultFormats, testconfig.GetTestConfig(afero.NewMemMapFs(), v))
    86	
    87	        for _, test := range []struct {
    88	                tp                media.Type
    89	                rawString         string
    90	                expectedMinString string
    91	                errorExpected     bool
    92	        }{
    93	                {media.Builtin.HTMLType, "<hello> Hugo! </hello>", "<hello> Hugo! </hello>", false},            // configured minifier
    94	                {media.Builtin.CSSType, " body { color: blue; }  ", "body{color:blue}", false},                 // default minifier
    95	                {media.Builtin.XMLType, " <hello>  Hugo!   </hello>  ", " <hello>  Hugo!   </hello>  ", false}, // disable Xml minification
    96	        } {
    97	                var b bytes.Buffer
    98	                if !test.errorExpected {
    99	                        c.Assert(m.Minify(test.tp, &b, strings.NewReader(test.rawString)), qt.IsNil)
   100	                        c.Assert(b.String(), qt.Equals, test.expectedMinString)
   101	                } else {
   102	                        err := m.Minify(test.tp, &b, strings.NewReader(test.rawString))
   103	                        c.Assert(err, qt.ErrorMatches, "minifier does not exist for mimetype")
   104	                }
   105	        }
   106	}
   107	
   108	func TestJSONRoundTrip(t *testing.T) {
   109	        c := qt.New(t)
   110	        m, _ := minifiers.New(media.DefaultTypes, output.DefaultFormats, testconfig.GetTestConfig(nil, nil))
   111	
   112	        for _, test := range []string{`{
   113	    "glossary": {
   114	        "title": "example glossary",
   115	                "GlossDiv": {
   116	            "title": "S",
   117	                        "GlossList": {
   118	                "GlossEntry": {
   119	                    "ID": "SGML",
   120	                                        "SortAs": "SGML",
   121	                                        "GlossTerm": "Standard Generalized Markup Language",
   122	                                        "Acronym": "SGML",
   123	                                        "Abbrev": "ISO 8879:1986",
   124	                                        "GlossDef": {
   125	                        "para": "A meta-markup language, used to create markup languages such as DocBook.",
   126	                                                "GlossSeeAlso": ["GML", "XML"]
   127	                    },
   128	                                        "GlossSee": "markup"
   129	                }
   130	            }
   131	        }
   132	    }
   133	}`} {
   134	
   135	                var b bytes.Buffer
   136	                m1 := make(map[string]any)
   137	                m2 := make(map[string]any)
   138	                c.Assert(json.Unmarshal([]byte(test), &m1), qt.IsNil)
   139	                c.Assert(m.Minify(media.Builtin.JSONType, &b, strings.NewReader(test)), qt.IsNil)
   140	                c.Assert(json.Unmarshal(b.Bytes(), &m2), qt.IsNil)
   141	                c.Assert(m1, qt.DeepEquals, m2)
   142	        }
   143	}

   150	        for _, test := range []struct {
   151	                tp                media.Type
   152	                rawString         string
   153	                expectedMinString string
   154	        }{
   155	                // Issue 5506
   156	                {media.Builtin.CSSType, " body { color: rgba(000, 000, 000, 0.7); }", "body{color:rgba(0,0,0,.7)}"},

   159	                // Issue #13082
   160	                {media.Builtin.HTMLType, "<gcse:searchresults-only></gcse:searchresults-only>", `<gcse:searchresults-only></gcse:searchresults-only>`},
   161	        } {
   162	                var b bytes.Buffer
   163	
   164	                c.Assert(m.Minify(test.tp, &b, strings.NewReader(test.rawString)), qt.IsNil)
   165	                c.Assert(b.String(), qt.Equals, test.expectedMinString)
   166	        }
   167	}

    14	package minifier
    15	
    16	import (
    17	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/minifiers"
    18	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/resources"
    19	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/resources/internal"
    20	        "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/resources/resource"
    21	)
    22	
    23	// Client for minification of Resource objects. Supported minifiers are:
    24	// css, html, js, json, svg and xml.
    25	type Client struct {
    26	        rs *resources.Spec
    27	        m  minifiers.Client
    28	}
    29	
    30	// New creates a new Client given a specification. Note that it is the media types
    31	// configured for the site that is used to match files to the correct minifier.
    32	func New(rs *resources.Spec) (*Client, error) {
    33	        m, err := minifiers.New(rs.MediaTypes(), rs.OutputFormats(), rs.Cfg)
    34	        if err != nil {
    35	                return nil, err
    36	        }
    37	        return &Client{rs: rs, m: m}, nil
    38	}
    39	
    40	type minifyTransformation struct {
    41	        rs *resources.Spec
    42	        m  minifiers.Client
    43	}
    44	
    45	func (t *minifyTransformation) Key() internal.ResourceTransformationKey {
    46	        return internal.NewResourceTransformationKey("minify")
    47	}
    48	
    49	func (t *minifyTransformation) Transform(ctx *resources.ResourceTransformationCtx) error {
    50	        ctx.AddOutPathIdentifier(".min")
    51	        return t.m.Minify(ctx.InMediaType, ctx.To, ctx.From)
    52	}
    53	
    54	func (c *Client) Minify(res resources.ResourceTransformer) (resource.Resource, error) {
    55	        return res.Transform(&minifyTransformation{
    56	                rs: c.rs,
    57	                m:  c.m,
    58	        })
    59	}
    60

    15	// Default minifiers for CSS, HTML, XML, JS, JSON, and XML
    16	var Default *minify.M
    17	
    18	func init() {
    19	        Default = minify.New()
    20	        Default.AddFunc("text/css", css.Minify)
    21	        Default.AddFunc("text/html", html.Minify)
    22	        Default.AddFunc("image/svg+xml", svg.Minify)
    23	        Default.AddFuncRegexp(regexp.MustCompile("^(application|text)/(x-)?(java|ecma|j|live)script(1\\.[0-5])?$|^module$"), js.Minify)
    24	        Default.AddFuncRegexp(regexp.MustCompile("[/+]json$"), json.Minify)
    25	        Default.AddFuncRegexp(regexp.MustCompile("[/+]xml$"), xml.Minify)
    26	
    27	        Default.AddFunc("importmap", json.Minify)
    28	        Default.AddFunc("speculationrules", json.Minify)
    29	
    30	        aspMinifier := &html.Minifier{}
    31	        aspMinifier.TemplateDelims = [2]string{"<%", "%>"}
    32	        Default.Add("text/asp", aspMinifier)
    33	        Default.Add("text/x-ejs-template", aspMinifier)
    34	
    35	        phpMinifier := &html.Minifier{}
    36	        phpMinifier.TemplateDelims = [2]string{"<?", "?>"} // also handles <?php
    37	        Default.Add("application/x-httpd-php", phpMinifier)
    38	
    39	        tmplMinifier := &html.Minifier{}
    40	        tmplMinifier.TemplateDelims = [2]string{"{{", "}}"}
    41	        Default.Add("text/x-go-template", tmplMinifier)
    42	        Default.Add("text/x-mustache-template", tmplMinifier)
    43	        Default.Add("text/x-handlebars-template", tmplMinifier)
    44	}

    47	func CSS(s string) (string, error) {

    49	}

     1	// Package svg minifies SVG1.1 following the specifications at http://www.w3.org/TR/SVG11/.
     2	package svg
     3	
     4	import (
     5	        "bytes"
     6	        "io"
     7	
     8	        "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2"
     9	        "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2/css"
    10	        minifyXML "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2/xml"
    11	        "github.com/tdewolff/parse/v2"
    12	        "github.com/tdewolff/parse/v2/buffer"
    13	        "github.com/tdewolff/parse/v2/xml"
    14	)
    15	
    16	var (
    17	        voidBytes        = []byte("/>")
    18	        isBytes          = []byte("=")
    19	        spaceBytes       = []byte(" ")
    20	        cdataEndBytes    = []byte("]]>")
    21	        zeroBytes        = []byte("0")
    22	        svgStartTagBytes = []byte("<svg")
    23	        cssMimeBytes     = []byte("text/css")
    24	        noneBytes        = []byte("none")
    25	        urlBytes         = []byte("url(")
    26	)
    27	
    28	////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
    29	
    30	// Minifier is an SVG minifier.
    31	type Minifier struct {
    32	        KeepComments bool
    33	        Precision    int // number of significant digits
    34	        newPrecision int // precision for new numbers
    35	        inline       bool
    36	}
    37	
    38	// Minify minifies SVG data, it reads from r and writes to w.
    39	func Minify(m *minify.M, w io.Writer, r io.Reader, params map[string]string) error {
    40	        return (&Minifier{}).Minify(m, w, r, params)
    41	}
    42	
    43	// Minify minifies SVG data, it reads from r and writes to w.
    44	func (o *Minifier) Minify(m *minify.M, w io.Writer, r io.Reader, params map[string]string) error {
    45	        tmp := &Minifier{}
    46	        *tmp = *o
    47	        o = tmp
    48	
    49	        o.newPrecision = o.Precision
    50	        if o.newPrecision <= 0 || 15 < o.newPrecision {
    51	                o.newPrecision = 15 // minimum number of digits a double can represent exactly
    52	        }
    53	        if !o.inline {
    54	                o.inline = params != nil && params["inline"] == "1"
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        // namespaces to keep
    58	        namespaces := []Hash{Xlink}
    59	
    60	        var tag Hash
    61	        defaultStyleType := cssMimeBytes
    62	        defaultStyleParams := map[string]string(nil)
    63	        defaultInlineStyleParams := map[string]string{"inline": "1"}
    64	
    65	        p := NewPathData(o)
    66	        minifyBuffer := buffer.NewWriter(make([]byte, 0, 64))
    67	        attrByteBuffer := make([]byte, 0, 64)
    68	
    69	        z := parse.NewInput(r)
    70	        defer z.Restore()
    71	
    72	        l := xml.NewLexer(z)
    73	        tb := NewTokenBuffer(z, l)
    74	        for {
    75	                t := *tb.Shift()
    76	                switch t.TokenType {
    77	                case xml.ErrorToken:
    78	                        if _, err := w.Write(nil); err != nil {
    79	                                return err
    80	                        }
    81	                        if l.Err() == io.EOF {
    82	                                return nil
    83	                        }
    84	                        return l.Err()
    85	                case xml.CommentToken:
    86	                        if o.KeepComments {
    87	                                w.Write(t.Data)
    88	                        }
    89	                case xml.DOCTYPEToken:
    90	                        if len(t.Text) > 0 && t.Text[len(t.Text)-1] == ']' {
    91	                                w.Write(t.Data)
    92	                        }
    93	                case xml.TextToken:
    94	                        t.Data = parse.ReplaceMultipleWhitespaceAndEntities(t.Data, minifyXML.EntitiesMap, nil)
    95	                        t.Data = parse.TrimWhitespace(t.Data)
    96	
    97	                        if tag == Style && len(t.Data) > 0 {
    98	                                if err := m.MinifyMimetype(defaultStyleType, w, buffer.NewReader(t.Data), defaultStyleParams); err != nil {
    99	                                        if err != minify.ErrNotExist {
   100	                                                return minify.UpdateErrorPosition(err, z, t.Offset)
   101	                                        }
   102	                                        w.Write(t.Data)
   103	                                }
   104	                        } else {
   105	                                w.Write(t.Data)
   106	                        }
   107	                case xml.CDATAToken:
   108	                        if tag == Style {
   109	                                minifyBuffer.Reset()
   110	                                if err := m.MinifyMimetype(defaultStyleType, minifyBuffer, buffer.NewReader(t.Text), defaultStyleParams); err == nil {
   111	                                        t.Data = append(t.Data[:9], minifyBuffer.Bytes()...)
   112	                                        t.Text = t.Data[9:]
   113	                                        t.Data = append(t.Data, cdataEndBytes...)
   114	                                } else if err != minify.ErrNotExist {
   115	                                        return minify.UpdateErrorPosition(err, z, t.Offset)
   116	                                }
   117	                        }
   118	                        var useText bool
   119	                        if t.Text, useText = xml.EscapeCDATAVal(&attrByteBuffer, t.Text); useText {
   120	                                t.Text = parse.ReplaceMultipleWhitespace(t.Text)
   121	                                t.Text = parse.TrimWhitespace(t.Text)
   122	                                w.Write(t.Text)
   123	                        } else {
   124	                                w.Write(t.Data)
   125	                        }
   126	                case xml.StartTagPIToken:
   127	                        for {
   128	                                if t := *tb.Shift(); t.TokenType == xml.StartTagClosePIToken || t.TokenType == xml.ErrorToken {
   129	                                        break
   130	                                }
   131	                        }
   132	                case xml.StartTagToken:
   133	                        tag = t.Hash
   134	                        if tag == Metadata {
   135	                                t.Data = nil
   136	                        } else if colon := bytes.IndexByte(t.Text, ':'); colon != -1 {
   137	                                prefix := ToHash(t.Text[:colon])
   138	                                if prefix == Svg {
   139	                                        t.Data = append(t.Data[:1], t.Data[5:]...)
   140	                                } else {
   141	                                        // skip attributes in namespace (eg. inkscape or sodipodi)
   142	                                        keep := false
   143	                                        for _, ns := range namespaces {
   144	                                                if prefix == ns {
   145	                                                        keep = true
   146	                                                        break
   147	                                                }
   148	                                        }
   149	                                        if !keep {
   150	                                                t.Data = nil
   151	                                        }
   152	                                }
   153	                        } else if tag == Defs && tb.Peek(1).TokenType == xml.StartTagCloseVoidToken {
   154	                                // skip empty tags
   155	                                t.Data = nil
   156	                        }
   157	
   158	                        if t.Data == nil {
   159	                                skipTag(tb)
   160	                        } else {
   161	                                w.Write(t.Data)
   162	                        }
   163	                case xml.AttributeToken:
   164	                        if t.Text == nil { // data is nil when attribute has been removed
   165	                                continue
   166	                        }
   167	
   168	                        attr := t.Hash
   169	                        val := t.AttrVal
   170	                        if n, m := parse.Dimension(val); n+m == len(val) && attr != Version { // TODO: inefficient, temporary measure
   171	                                val, _ = o.shortenDimension(val)
   172	                        }
   173	                        if attr == Xml_Space && bytes.Equal(val, []byte("preserve")) ||
   174	                                tag == Svg && (o.inline && attr == Xmlns ||
   175	                                        attr == Version && bytes.Equal(val, []byte("1.1")) ||
   176	                                        attr == X && bytes.Equal(val, zeroBytes) ||
   177	                                        attr == Y && bytes.Equal(val, zeroBytes) ||
   178	                                        attr == PreserveAspectRatio && bytes.Equal(val, []byte("xMidYMid meet")) ||
   179	                                        attr == BaseProfile && bytes.Equal(val, noneBytes) ||
   180	                                        attr == ContentScriptType && bytes.Equal(val, []byte("application/ecmascript")) ||
   181	                                        attr == ContentStyleType && bytes.Equal(val, cssMimeBytes)) ||
   182	                                tag == Style && attr == Type && bytes.Equal(val, cssMimeBytes) {
   183	                                continue
   184	                        }
   185	
   186	                        // skip attributes in namespace (eg. inkscape or sodipodi)
   187	                        if colon := bytes.IndexByte(t.Text, ':'); colon != -1 {
   188	                                keep := false
   189	                                prefix, name := ToHash(t.Text[:colon]), ToHash(t.Text[colon+1:])
   190	                                for _, ns := range namespaces {
   191	                                        if prefix == ns || tag == Svg && prefix == Xmlns && name == ns {
   192	                                                keep = true
   193	                                                break
   194	                                        }
   195	                                }
   196	                                if !keep {
   197	                                        continue
   198	                                }
   199	                        }
   200	
   201	                        w.Write(spaceBytes)
   202	                        w.Write(t.Text)
   203	                        w.Write(isBytes)
   204	
   205	                        if tag == Svg && attr == ContentStyleType {
   206	                                val = minify.Mediatype(val)
   207	                                defaultStyleType = val
   208	                        } else if attr == Style {
   209	                                minifyBuffer.Reset()
   210	                                if err := m.MinifyMimetype(defaultStyleType, minifyBuffer, buffer.NewReader(val), defaultInlineStyleParams); err == nil {
   211	                                        val = minifyBuffer.Bytes()
   212	                                } else if err != minify.ErrNotExist {
   213	                                        return minify.UpdateErrorPosition(err, z, t.Offset)
   214	                                }
   215	                        } else if attr == D {
   216	                                val = p.ShortenPathData(val)
   217	                        } else if attr == ViewBox {
   218	                                j := 0
   219	                                newVal := val[:0]
   220	                                for i := 0; i < 4; i++ {
   221	                                        if i != 0 {
   222	                                                if j >= len(val) || val[j] != ' ' && val[j] != ',' {
   223	                                                        newVal = append(newVal, val[j:]...)
   224	                                                        break
   225	                                                }
   226	                                                newVal = append(newVal, ' ')
   227	                                                j++
   228	                                        }
   229	                                        if dim, n := o.shortenDimension(val[j:]); n > 0 {
   230	                                                newVal = append(newVal, dim...)
   231	                                                j += n
   232	                                        } else {
   233	                                                newVal = append(newVal, val[j:]...)
   234	                                                break
   235	                                        }
   236	                                }
   237	                                val = newVal
   238	                        } else if colorAttrMap[attr] && len(val) > 0 && (len(val) < 5 || !parse.EqualFold(val[:4], urlBytes)) {
   239	                                //parse.ToLower(val)
   240	                                if val[0] == '#' {
   241	                                        if name, ok := css.ShortenColorHex[string(val)]; ok {
   242	                                                val = name
   243	                                        } else if len(val) == 7 && val[1] == val[2] && val[3] == val[4] && val[5] == val[6] {
   244	                                                val[2] = val[3]
   245	                                                val[3] = val[5]
   246	                                                val = val[:4]
   247	                                        }
   248	                                } else if hex, ok := css.ShortenColorName[css.ToHash(val)]; ok {
   249	                                        val = hex
   250	                                        // } else if len(val) > 5 && bytes.Equal(val[:4], []byte("rgb(")) && val[len(val)-1] == ')' {
   251	                                        // TODO: handle rgb(x, y, z) and hsl(x, y, z)
   252	                                }
   253	                        }
   254	
   255	                        // prefer single or double quotes depending on what occurs more often in value
   256	                        val = xml.EscapeAttrVal(&attrByteBuffer, val)
   257	                        w.Write(val)
   258	                case xml.StartTagCloseToken:
   259	                        next := tb.Peek(0)
   260	                        skipExtra := false
   261	                        if next.TokenType == xml.TextToken && parse.IsAllWhitespace(next.Data) {
   262	                                next = tb.Peek(1)
   263	                                skipExtra = true
   264	                        }
   265	                        if next.TokenType == xml.EndTagToken {
   266	                                // collapse empty tags to single void tag
   267	                                tb.Shift()
   268	                                if skipExtra {
   269	                                        tb.Shift()
   270	                                }
   271	                                w.Write(voidBytes)
   272	                        } else {
   273	                                w.Write(t.Data)
   274	                        }
   275	
   276	                        if tag == ForeignObject {
   277	                                printTag(w, tb, tag)
   278	                        }
   279	                case xml.StartTagCloseVoidToken:
   280	                        tag = 0
   281	                        w.Write(t.Data)
   282	                case xml.EndTagToken:
   283	                        tag = 0
   284	                        if len(t.Data) > 3+len(t.Text) {
   285	                                t.Data[2+len(t.Text)] = '>'
   286	                                t.Data = t.Data[:3+len(t.Text)]
   287	                        }
   288	                        w.Write(t.Data)
   289	                }
   290	        }
   291	}
   292	
   293	func (o *Minifier) shortenDimension(b []byte) ([]byte, int) {
   294	        if n, m := parse.Dimension(b); n > 0 {
   295	                unit := b[n : n+m]
   296	                b = minify.Number(b[:n], o.Precision)
   297	                if len(b) != 1 || b[0] != '0' {
   298	                        if m == 2 && unit[0] == 'p' && unit[1] == 'x' {
   299	                                unit = nil
   300	                        } else if m > 1 { // only percentage is length 1
   301	                                parse.ToLower(unit)
   302	                        }
   303	                        b = append(b, unit...)
   304	                }
   305	                return b, n + m
   306	        }
   307	        return b, 0
   308	}
   309	
   310	////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
   311	
   312	func printTag(w io.Writer, tb *TokenBuffer, tag Hash) {
   313	        level := 0
   314	        inStartTag := false
   315	        for {
   316	                t := *tb.Peek(0)
   317	                switch t.TokenType {
   318	                case xml.ErrorToken:
   319	                        return
   320	                case xml.StartTagToken:
   321	                        inStartTag = t.Hash == tag
   322	                        if t.Hash == tag {
   323	                                level++
   324	                        }
   325	                case xml.StartTagCloseVoidToken:
   326	                        if inStartTag {
   327	                                if level == 0 {
   328	                                        return
   329	                                }
   330	                                level--
   331	                        }
   332	                case xml.EndTagToken:
   333	                        if t.Hash == tag {
   334	                                if level == 0 {
   335	                                        return
   336	                                }
   337	                                level--
   338	                        }
   339	                }
   340	                w.Write(t.Data)
   341	                tb.Shift()
   342	        }
   343	}
   344	
   345	func skipTag(tb *TokenBuffer) {
   346	        level := 0
   347	        for {
   348	                if t := *tb.Shift(); t.TokenType == xml.ErrorToken {
   349	                        break
   350	                } else if t.TokenType == xml.EndTagToken || t.TokenType == xml.StartTagCloseVoidToken {
   351	                        if level == 0 {
   352	                                break
   353	                        }
   354	                        level--
   355	                } else if t.TokenType == xml.StartTagToken {
   356	                        level++
   357	                }
   358	        }
   359	}
   360

   240	// String returns the text associated with the hash.
   241	func (i Hash) String() string {
   242	        return string(i.Bytes())
   243	}
   244	
   245	// Bytes returns the text associated with the hash.
   246	func (i Hash) Bytes() []byte {
   247	        start := uint32(i >> 8)
   248	        n := uint32(i & 0xff)
   249	        if start+n > uint32(len(_Hash_text)) {
   250	                return []byte{}
   251	        }
   252	        return _Hash_text[start : start+n]
   253	}
   254	
   255	// ToHash returns a hash Hash for a given []byte. Hash is a uint32 that is associated with the text in []byte. It returns zero if no match found.
   256	func ToHash(s []byte) Hash {
   257	        if len(s) == 0 || len(s) > _Hash_maxLen {
   258	                return 0
   259	        }
   260	        //if 3 < len(s) {
   261	        //      return HashMap[string(s)]
   262	        //}
   263	        h := uint32(_Hash_hash0)
   264	        for i := 0; i < len(s); i++ {
   265	                h ^= uint32(s[i])
   266	                h *= 16777619
   267	        }
   268	        if i := _Hash_table[h&uint32(len(_Hash_table)-1)]; int(i&0xff) == len(s) {
   269	                t := _Hash_text[i>>8 : i>>8+i&0xff]
   270	                for i := 0; i < len(s); i++ {
   271	                        if t[i] != s[i] {
   272	                                goto NEXT
   273	                        }
   274	                }
   275	                return i
   276	        }
   277	NEXT:
   278	        if i := _Hash_table[(h>>16)&uint32(len(_Hash_table)-1)]; int(i&0xff) == len(s) {
   279	                t := _Hash_text[i>>8 : i>>8+i&0xff]
   280	                for i := 0; i < len(s); i++ {
   281	                        if t[i] != s[i] {
   282	                                return 0
   283	                        }
   284	                }
   285	                return i
   286	        }
   287	        return 0
   288	}
   289	
   290	const _Hash_hash0 = 0x822145e
   291	const _Hash_maxLen = 28
   292

   294	        "baseProfiletter-spacinglyph-orientation-verticalignment-base" +

   306	        "oke-opacitystroke-widthsvgswitchsymbolunicode-bidirectionuse" +

   308	        "ord-spacingwriting-modefsolid-opacityxlinkxml:spacexmlnstop-" +
   309	        "opacity")
   310	
   311	var _Hash_table = [1 << 8]Hash{
   312	        0x2:  0x1140b, // font-family
   313	        0x7:  0xc602,  // ry
   314	        0xa:  0x2180f, // shape-rendering
   315	        0xb:  0x1c308, // metadata
   316	        0xc:  0x9807,  // display
   317	        0x11: 0x31907, // version
   318	        0x1a: 0x37f0c, // stop-opacity

   320	        0x1c: 0x2690b, // white-space
   321	        0x1e: 0x710f,  // text-decoration
   322	        0x22: 0x17a0f, // image-rendering
   323	        0x26: 0xf70e,  // text-rendering
   324	        0x27: 0x37209, // xml:space
   325	        0x2a: 0x2f60c, // unicode-bidi
   326	        0x2b: 0x14204, // href

   204	func TestWriterErrors(t *testing.T) {
   205	        errorTests := []struct {
   206	                svg string
   207	                n   []int
   208	        }{
   209	                {`<!DOCTYPE svg PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD SVG 1.1//EN" "foo.dtd" [ <!ENTITY x "bar"> ]>`, []int{0}},

   214	                {`<path d="x"/>`, []int{0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5}},
   215	                {`<path></path>`, []int{1}},
   216	                {`<svg>x</svg>`, []int{1, 3}},
   217	                {`<svg>x</svg >`, []int{3}},
   218	        }
   219	
   220	        m := minify.New()
   221	        for _, tt := range errorTests {
   222	                for _, n := range tt.n {
   223	                        t.Run(fmt.Sprint(tt.svg, " ", tt.n), func(t *testing.T) {
   224	                                r := bytes.NewBufferString(tt.svg)
   225	                                w := test.NewErrorWriter(n)
   226	                                err := Minify(m, w, r, nil)
   227	                                test.T(t, err, test.ErrPlain)
   228	                        })
   229	                }
   230	        }
   231	}
   232	
   233	func TestMinifyErrors(t *testing.T) {
   234	        errorTests := []struct {
   235	                svg string
   236	                err error
   237	        }{
   238	                {`<style>abc</style>`, test.ErrPlain},
   239	                {`<style><![CDATA[abc]]></style>`, test.ErrPlain},
   240	                {`<path style="abc"/>`, test.ErrPlain},
   241	        }
   242	
   243	        m := minify.New()
   244	        m.AddFunc("text/css", func(_ *minify.M, w io.Writer, r io.Reader, _ map[string]string) error {
   245	                return test.ErrPlain
   246	        })
   247	        for _, tt := range errorTests {
   248	                t.Run(tt.svg, func(t *testing.T) {
   249	                        r := bytes.NewBufferString(tt.svg)
   250	                        w := &bytes.Buffer{}
   251	                        err := Minify(m, w, r, nil)
   252	                        test.T(t, err, tt.err)
   253	                })
   254	        }
   255	}
   256	
   257	////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
   258	
   259	func ExampleMinify() {
   260	        m := minify.New()
   261	        m.AddFunc("image/svg+xml", Minify)
   262	        m.AddFunc("text/css", css.Minify)
   263	
   264	        if err := m.Minify("image/svg+xml", os.Stdout, os.Stdin); err != nil {
   265	                panic(err)
   266	        }
   267	}
   268

package main

import (
    "bytes"
    "fmt"
    
    "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2"
    "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2/svg"
    "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2/css"
    "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2/html"
    "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2/js"
    "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2/json"
    "github.com/tdewolff/minify/v2/xml"
)

func main() {
    m := minify.New()
    m.AddFunc("text/css", css.Minify)
    m.AddFunc("text/html", html.Minify)
    m.AddFunc("image/svg+xml", svg.Minify)
    m.AddFuncRegexp(regexp.MustCompile("^(application|text)/(x-)?(java|ecma|j|live)script(1\\.[0-5])?$|^module$"), js.Minify)
    m.AddFuncRegexp(regexp.MustCompile("[/+]json$"), json.Minify)
    m.AddFuncRegexp(regexp.MustCompile("[/+]xml$"), xml.Minify)

    tests := []struct {
        input    string
        expected string
    }{
        // AlpineJS bindings
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-data="{show: true}" @click="show = !show"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-data="{show: true}" @click="show = !show"/></svg>`},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect :class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect :class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-bind:class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-bind:class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-on:click.prevent="show = !show"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-on:click.prevent="show = !show"/></svg>`},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-transition:enter="fade"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-transition:enter="fade"/></svg>`},
        // Standard attributes should still work
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect width="100" height="100"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect width="100" height="100"/></svg>`},
        // Issue: SVG with custom attributes like @click
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect @click="handle()"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect @click="handle()"/></svg>`},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect @something="value"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect @something="value"/></svg>`},
    }

    for _, tt := range tests {
        r := bytes.NewBufferString(tt.input)
        w := &bytes.Buffer{}
        err := svg.Minify(m, w, r, nil)
        if err != nil {
            fmt.Printf("ERROR: %v\n", err)
        }
        result := w.String()
        if result != tt.expected {
            fmt.Printf("FAIL:\n  input:    %s\n  expected: %s\n  got:      %s\n", tt.input, tt.expected, result)
        } else {
            fmt.Printf("PASS: %s\n", tt.input)
        }
    }
}
EOF

Interesting! So the issue is clear now. The SVG minifier is stripping attributes that have a colon in them, like `:class`, `x-bind:class`, `x-on:click.prevent`, `x-transition:enter`. It's treating them as namespaced attributes (like `inkscape:foo`) and stripping them because they're not in the allowed namespaces list.

Looking at the code in svg.go, the logic at line 187-199 handles attributes with a colon:
```go
if colon := bytes.IndexByte(t.Text, ':'); colon != -1 {
    keep := false
    prefix, name := ToHash(t.Text[:colon]), ToHash(t.Text[colon+1:])
    for _, ns := range namespaces {
        if prefix == ns || tag == Svg && prefix == Xmlns && name == ns {
            keep = true
            break
        }
    }
    if !keep {
        continue
    }
}
```

The `namespaces` variable is initialized to just `[Hash{Xlink}]` at line 58. So any attribute with a colon that doesn't have the prefix `xlink` gets stripped. This breaks AlpineJS bindings like `x-bind:class`, `x-on:click`, `x-transition:enter`, `:class` (colon prefix), etc.

But wait, let me check what happens with `:class` - the prefix would be empty string. Let me trace through the code:

For `:class`:
- `colon := bytes.IndexByte(t.Text, ':')` → 0
- `prefix := ToHash(t.Text[:0])` → `ToHash([]byte{})` → 0 (empty, returns 0)
- `name := ToHash(t.Text[1:])` → hash of "class"

Then `prefix == ns` would be `0 == Hash{Xlink}` which is false, so it's skipped.

For `x-bind:class`:
- `colon` is at position 6
- `prefix := ToHash(t.Text[:6])` → hash of "x-bind"
- This hash is not in the namespaces list, so it gets stripped.

Now the issue is: the SVG minifier should not strip attributes with colons that are not part of known SVG namespaces. But the problem is that there are many valid uses of colons in attributes:
1. AlpineJS directives: `x-bind:class`, `x-on:click`, `x-transition:enter`, `:class` (shorthand)
2. Vue.js bindings: similar
3. Other framework bindings

The fix in the Hugo context would be to update the SVG minifier to not strip attributes with colons, or to pass custom namespaces to keep. But wait, looking at the tdewolff/minify library, the issue is probably in that library itself.

Let me check if there's a more recent version of the minify library that fixes this. But the PR description says the issue is about the SVG minifier being broken for AlpineJS bindings, and the reference is to tdewolff/minify issue #936.

Let me check what the latest version is. But maybe the issue is that the SVG minifier should not strip attributes that have a colon at all, unless they're in a list of known "bad" namespaces. Let me look at the tdewolff/minify source more to understand the intended behavior:

Actually, let me look at the behavior with the prefix `x-bind`:

Looking at the SVG minifier code at line 187-199:
```go
if colon := bytes.IndexByte(t.Text, ':'); colon != -1 {
    keep := false
    prefix, name := ToHash(t.Text[:colon]), ToHash(t.Text[colon+1:])
    for _, ns := range namespaces {
        if prefix == ns || tag == Svg && prefix == Xmlns && name == ns {
            keep = true
            break
        }
    }
    if !keep {
        continue
    }
}
```

This checks if the prefix is in the `namespaces` list. The `namespaces` list is `[Hash{Xlink}]`. 

But wait, there's a subtlety: What about attributes that have a colon but the prefix is NOT a known namespace? The issue is that for AlpineJS, `x-bind:class` has prefix `x-bind` which is not in the namespaces list, so it gets stripped. But `x-data` (no colon) works fine.

The problem is that the SVG minifier is over-aggressive in stripping unknown namespaced attributes. It should probably keep all attributes except those in known "bad" namespaces (like `inkscape`, `sodipodi`, etc.), or at least provide a way to configure additional namespaces to keep.

But wait, looking at the test case at line 64:
```go
{`<xyz:rect width="100%" height="100%" fill="green"/>`, ``},
```
This shows that unknown namespace prefixes should be removed. But the problem is that AlpineJS uses colon-based attributes that aren't XML namespaces at all!

The fundamental issue is: attributes like `:class` and `x-bind:class` are NOT XML namespaced attributes - they're framework-specific directives. The SVG minifier incorrectly treats any attribute with a colon as an XML namespace prefix and strips it if it's not in the allowed list.

So the fix should be in the tdewolff/minify library. Let me check if there's a way to update this. But perhaps the PR description is about a fix that needs to be made in Hugo's configuration - maybe Hugo should update its dependency or configure the SVG minifier differently.

2. Namespaces are now `[][]byte` instead of `[]Hash`
3. The comparison uses `bytes.Equal` instead of hash comparison

But there's still the issue: if the prefix is empty (like `:class`), then `t.Text[:0]` is an empty byte slice. The namespace list is `[[]byte("xlink")]`, so an empty prefix won't match. This means `:class` would still be stripped!

Let me test this with the updated library:

Wait, I already tested with v2.24.13 and `:class` still got stripped. Let me check if there's a way to also keep the empty prefix. Let me look at the updated SVG minifier more carefully:

    45	// Minify minifies SVG data, it reads from r and writes to w.
    46	func (o *Minifier) Minify(m *minify.M, w io.Writer, r io.Reader, params map[string]string) error {
    47	        tmp := &Minifier{}
    48	        *tmp = *o
    49	        o = tmp
    50	
    51	        o.newPrecision = o.Precision
    52	        if o.newPrecision <= 0 || 15 < o.newPrecision {
    53	                o.newPrecision = 15 // minimum number of digits a double can represent exactly
    54	        }
    55	        if !o.inline {
    56	                o.inline = params != nil && params["inline"] == "1"
    57	        }
    58	
    59	        // namespaces to keep
    60	        namespaces := [][]byte{[]byte("xlink")}

    62	                namespaces = append(namespaces, []byte(ns))
    63	        }

    80	                t := *tb.Shift()
    81	                switch t.TokenType {
    82	                case xml.ErrorToken:
    83	                        if _, err := w.Write(nil); err != nil {
    84	                                return err
    85	                        }
    86	                        if l.Err() == io.EOF {
    87	                                return nil
    88	                        }
    89	                        return l.Err()
    90	                case xml.CommentToken:
    91	                        if o.KeepComments {
    92	                                w.Write(t.Data)
    93	                        }
    94	                case xml.DOCTYPEToken:

    96	                                w.Write(t.Data)
    97	                        }

   100	                        t.Data = parse.TrimWhitespace(t.Data)

   105	                                                return minify.UpdateErrorPosition(err, z, t.Offset)
   106	                                        }
   107	                                        w.Write(t.Data)
   108	                                }

   297	func (o *Minifier) shortenDimension(b []byte) ([]byte, int) {
   298	        if n, m := parse.Dimension(b); n > 0 {
   299	                unit := b[n : n+m]
   300	                b = minify.Number(b[:n], o.Precision)
   301	                if len(b) != 1 || b[0] != '0' {
   302	                        if m == 2 && unit[0] == 'p' && unit[1] == 'x' {
   303	                                unit = nil
   304	                        } else if m > 1 { // only percentage is length 1
   305	                                parse.ToLower(unit)
   306	                        }
   307	                        b = append(b, unit...)
   308	                }
   309	                return b, n + m
   310	        }
   311	        return b, 0
   312	}
   313

   315	
   316	func printTag(w io.Writer, tb *TokenBuffer, tag Hash) {
   317	        level := 0
   318	        inStartTag := false
   319	        for {
   320	                t := *tb.Peek(0)
   321	                switch t.TokenType {
   322	                case xml.ErrorToken:
   323	                        return
   324	                case xml.StartTagToken:
   325	                        inStartTag = t.Hash == tag
   326	                        if t.Hash == tag {
   327	                                level++
   328	                        }
   329	                case xml.StartTagCloseVoidToken:
   330	                        if inStartTag {
   331	                                if level == 0 {
   332	                                        return
   333	                                }
   334	                                level--
   335	                        }
   336	                case xml.EndTagToken:
   337	                        if t.Hash == tag {
   338	                                if level == 0 {
   339	                                        return
   340	                                }
   341	                                level--
   342	                        }
   343	                }
   344	                w.Write(t.Data)
   345	                tb.Shift()
   346	        }
   347	}
   348	
   349	func skipTag(tb *TokenBuffer) {
   350	        level := 0
   351	        for {
   352	                if t := *tb.Shift(); t.TokenType == xml.ErrorToken {
   353	                        break
   354	                } else if t.TokenType == xml.EndTagToken || t.TokenType == xml.StartTagCloseVoidToken {
   355	                        if level == 0 {
   356	                                break
   357	                        }
   358	                        level--
   359	                } else if t.TokenType == xml.StartTagToken {
   360	                        level++
   361	                }
   362	        }
   363	}

So the updated SVG minifier in v2.24.13 adds `KeepNamespaces` field but still has the same problem: it strips attributes with colons that are not in the namespaces list. The namespace list includes only `xlink` by default. 

However, looking at this, I notice that the issue is specifically about Hugo needing to:
1. Update the minify dependency to a version that has `KeepNamespaces`
2. Configure the SVG minifier to keep AlpineJS-related namespaces (like `x-on`, `x-bind`, etc.) or better yet, keep ALL unknown namespaces

But wait, the problem is more fundamental: even with `KeepNamespaces`, the `:class` (empty prefix) case won't work because an empty prefix `""` won't match anything.

Let me think about what the proper fix should be. Looking at the issue referenced (tdewolff/minify#936), the fix in the library should probably be to NOT strip attributes where the prefix is not a known "bad" namespace. In other words, only strip attributes from known namespaces like `inkscape`, `sodipodi`, etc., and keep everything else.

But since we're working on the Hugo repo, and the library already has `KeepNamespaces` in the newer version, maybe the fix is:
1. Update to the newer version of tdewolff/minify
2. Add support for `KeepNamespaces` in Hugo's minifier configuration

But I also need to consider that `:class` (empty prefix) won't be saved even with `KeepNamespaces`. Let me look at the library code more carefully to see if there's a way to handle this.

Actually, looking at the code at lines 192-203:
```go
// skip attributes in namespace (eg. inkscape or sodipodi)
if colon := bytes.IndexByte(t.Text, ':'); colon != -1 {
    keep := false
    for _, ns := range namespaces {
        if bytes.Equal(t.Text[:colon], ns) || tag == Svg && bytes.Equal(t.Text[:colon], xmlnsBytes) && bytes.Equal(ns, t.Text[colon+1:]) {
            keep = true
            break
        }
    }
    if !keep {
        continue
    }
}
```

For `:class`, `colon` is 0, so `t.Text[:0]` is an empty byte slice. The loop checks if any namespace equals the empty slice - none do (xlink is not empty). So it falls through to `continue` and the attribute is skipped.

To fix this properly, the library should handle the case where `colon == 0` (empty prefix) and keep the attribute. But we can't modify the library directly.

Let me check if there's a version with a fix for issue #936. The issue is about AlpineJS bindings. Let me look at the latest changes to the SVG minifier:

Looking at the diff we already saw between v2.24.10 and v2.24.13:
1. Added `KeepNamespaces` field
2. Changed from hash-based to bytes-based comparison
3. Added `xmlnsBytes` constant

But the fundamental issue remains: the empty prefix case (`:class`) is not handled. 

Maybe the fix needs to be in Hugo's code to configure the minifier properly. Let me think about this differently:

The Hugo project can fix this by:
1. Updating to the latest tdewolff/minify that has `KeepNamespaces`
2. Setting `KeepNamespaces` to include common AlpineJS prefixes AND an empty string for the `:attr` shorthand

But wait, looking at the minifier configuration in Hugo, the `SVG` struct is used directly from the library. Hugo needs to add a configuration option for `KeepNamespaces` in the SVG minifier config.

Let me check if there's a way to pass an empty string as a namespace to keep all attributes with colons. Actually, looking at the library code:

```go
namespaces := [][]byte{[]byte("xlink")}
for _, ns := range o.KeepNamespaces {
    namespaces = append(namespaces, []byte(ns))
}
```

If we pass an empty string `""` as a namespace, then `[]byte("")` would be an empty byte slice, and the `bytes.Equal(t.Text[:colon], ns)` check would match when `colon == 0` (i.e., for `:class`). That would fix the `:class` case!

So the fix could be:
1. Update to tdewolff/minify v2.24.13 (or later)
2. In Hugo's minifier config, set `KeepNamespaces` for SVG to include common AlpineJS/Vue prefixes like `x-on`, `x-bind`, `x-transition`, `x-effect`, etc., and also include an empty string `""` to handle the `:attr` shorthand.

But actually, this approach is fragile because there could be many different prefixes used by different frameworks. A more robust approach would be to fix the library to not strip unknown namespaced attributes at all, but that's not under our control.

Let me look at this from another angle: maybe the fix is to update the dependency to a version that has the fix, and then update Hugo's default configuration for the SVG minifier to include common AlpineJS/Vue prefixes.

Let me first restore the original go.mod and then make the necessary changes:

3. The `KeepNamespaces` field should be configurable through Hugo's config

But actually, looking at this more carefully, I think the proper fix is:
1. Update the dependency (already done)
2. In the default configuration for SVG, set `KeepNamespaces` to include an empty string (to preserve `:attr` shorthand) and common framework prefixes

    74	func TestConfigureMinify(t *testing.T) {
    75	        c := qt.New(t)
    76	        v := config.New()
    77	        v.Set("minify", map[string]any{
    78	                "disablexml": true,
    79	                "tdewolff": map[string]any{
    80	                        "html": map[string]any{
    81	                                "keepwhitespace": true,
    82	                        },
    83	                },
    84	        })
    85	        m, _ := minifiers.New(media.DefaultTypes, output.DefaultFormats, testconfig.GetTestConfig(afero.NewMemMapFs(), v))
    86	
    87	        for _, test := range []struct {
    88	                tp                media.Type
    89	                rawString         string
    90	                expectedMinString string
    91	                errorExpected     bool
    92	        }{
    93	                {media.Builtin.HTMLType, "<hello> Hugo! </hello>", "<hello> Hugo! </hello>", false},            // configured minifier
    94	                {media.Builtin.CSSType, " body { color: blue; }  ", "body{color:blue}", false},                 // default minifier
    95	                {media.Builtin.XMLType, " <hello>  Hugo!   </hello>  ", " <hello>  Hugo!   </hello>  ", false}, // disable Xml minification
    96	        } {
    97	                var b bytes.Buffer
    98	                if !test.errorExpected {
    99	                        c.Assert(m.Minify(test.tp, &b, strings.NewReader(test.rawString)), qt.IsNil)
   100	                        c.Assert(b.String(), qt.Equals, test.expectedMinString)
   101	                } else {
   102	                        err := m.Minify(test.tp, &b, strings.NewReader(test.rawString))
   103	                        c.Assert(err, qt.ErrorMatches, "minifier does not exist for mimetype")
   104	                }
   105	        }
   106	}

    44	                        classess = strings.Split(classes, " ")
    45	                }

   166	func TestEndsWithTag(t *testing.T) {
   167	        c := qt.New((t))
   168	
   169	        for _, test := range []struct {
   170	                name    string
   171	                s       string
   172	                tagName string
   173	                expect  bool
   174	        }{
   175	                {"empty", "", "div", false},
   176	                {"no match", "foo", "div", false},
   177	                {"no close", "foo<div>", "div", false},
   178	                {"no close 2", "foo/div>", "div", false},
   179	                {"no close 2", "foo//div>", "div", false},
   180	                {"no tag", "foo</>", "div", false},
   181	                {"match", "foo</div>", "div", true},
   182	                {"match space", "foo<  / div>", "div", true},
   183	                {"match space 2", "foo<  / div   \n>", "div", true},
   184	                {"match case", "foo</DIV>", "div", true},
   185	                {"self closing", `</defs><g><g><path fill="#010101" d=asdf"/>`, "div", false},
   186	        } {
   187	                c.Run(test.name, func(c *qt.C) {
   188	                        got := isClosedByTag([]byte(test.s), []byte(test.tagName))
   189	                        c.Assert(got, qt.Equals, test.expect)
   190	                })
   191	        }
   192	}

But what values should be in `KeepNamespaces`? Looking at the AlpineJS documentation and the tests in `publisher/htmlElementsCollector_test.go`, the common prefixes are:
- `x-bind` (for `x-bind:class`, `x-bind:href`, etc.)
- `x-on` (for `x-on:click`, etc.)
- `x-transition` (for `x-transition:enter`, etc.)
- `v-bind` (Vue.js)
- Empty string `""` for the shorthand `:class`, `:href`, etc.

        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-transition:enter="fade"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-transition:enter="fade"/></svg>`, []string{"", "x-bind", "x-on", "x-transition"}},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-data="{show: true}" @click="show = !show"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-data="{show: true}" @click="show = !show"/></svg>`, []string{"", "x-bind", "x-on", "x-transition"}},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect v-bind:class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect v-bind:class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`, []string{"", "x-bind", "x-on", "x-transition", "v-bind"}},
    }

    for _, tt := range tests {
        m := minify.New()
        o := &svg.Minifier{KeepNamespaces: tt.keepNS}
        r := bytes.NewBufferString(tt.input)
        w := &bytes.Buffer{}
        err := o.Minify(m, w, r, nil)
        if err != nil {
            fmt.Printf("ERROR: %v\n", err)
        }
        result := w.String()
        if result != tt.expected {
            fmt.Printf("FAIL:\n  input:    %s\n  expected: %s\n  got:      %s\n", tt.input, tt.expected, result)
        } else {
            fmt.Printf("PASS: %s\n", tt.input)
        }
    }
}

1. Update the default SVG minifier configuration to include these namespace prefixes
2. Make sure the configuration can be customized by users

Let me look at the current configuration again:

In `/testbed/minifiers/config.go`, the `defaultTdewolffConfig` has:
```go
SVG: svg.Minifier{
    KeepComments: false,
    Precision:    0, // 0 means no trimming
},
```

I need to add `KeepNamespaces` to this default configuration. But what should the default list be? Looking at common frontend frameworks:
- AlpineJS: `x-bind`, `x-on`, `x-transition`, `:attr` (empty prefix)
- Vue.js: `v-bind`, `v-on`
- Also maybe `x-effect`, `x-model`, `x-show`, `x-text`, `x-html`, `x-ref`, `x-cloak`, `x-teleport`, `x-if`, `x-for`

But `x-data`, `x-effect`, `x-model`, etc. don't have a colon, so they already work fine. Only the ones with a colon need to be in KeepNamespaces.

Let me check the AlpineJS documentation to see the full list of directives that use colons:
- `x-on:event` (event listener)
- `x-bind:attr` (attribute binding)
- `x-transition:phase` (transition phases)
- `:attr` is shorthand for `x-bind:attr`
- `@event` is shorthand for `x-on:event` (no colon, already works)

For Vue.js:
- `v-bind:attr`
- `v-on:event`
- `v-slot:name`
- `v-cloak` (no colon)

I think a reasonable default would be to include empty string and the common prefixes. Let me check what the Hugo project would want to include. Given the test file in `publisher/htmlElementsCollector_test.go` already has tests for AlpineJS bindings and Vue bind, the default should include at least:
- `""` (empty, for `:attr` shorthand)
- `x-bind`
- `x-on`
- `x-transition`
- `v-bind`

Now let me make the changes to the Hugo source code:

1. First, update `minifiers/config.go` to add `KeepNamespaces` to the default SVG configuration
2. The `KeepNamespaces` field should be configurable via Hugo's config

Let me check if the config.go needs to handle new configuration fields. The `mapstructure.WeakDecode` is used to decode the configuration, so if the user adds a `keepnamespaces` field under `minify.tdewolff.svg`, it should automatically be mapped to the `KeepNamespaces` field in the `svg.Minifier` struct.

package main

import (
    "bytes"
    "fmt"
    
    "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/config"
    "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/config/testconfig"
    "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/media"

    "github.com/gohugoio/hugo/output"
)

func main() {
    m, _ := minifiers.New(media.DefaultTypes, output.DefaultFormats, testconfig.GetTestConfig(nil, nil))
    
    tests := []struct {
        input    string
        expected string
    }{
        // AlpineJS bindings
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-data="{show: true}" @click="show = !show"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-data="{show: true}" @click="show = !show"/></svg>`},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect :class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect :class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-bind:class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-bind:class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-on:click.prevent="show = !show"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-on:click.prevent="show = !show"/></svg>`},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-transition:enter="fade"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect x-transition:enter="fade"/></svg>`},
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect v-bind:class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect v-bind:class="{'active': isActive}"/></svg>`},
        // Standard attributes should still work
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect width="100" height="100"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><rect width="100" height="100"/></svg>`},
        // xlink should still work
        {`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><use xlink:href="#myIcon"/></svg>`, `<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><use xlink:href="#myIcon"/></svg>`},
    }

    for _, tt := range tests {
        var b bytes.Buffer
        err := m.Minify(media.Builtin.SVGType, &b, bytes.NewBufferString(tt.input))
        if err != nil {
            fmt.Printf("ERROR: %v\n", err)
        }
        result := b.String()
        if result != tt.expected {
            fmt.Printf("FAIL:\n  input:    %s\n  expected: %s\n  got:      %s\n", tt.input, tt.expected, result)
        } else {
            fmt.Printf("PASS: %s\n", tt.input)
        }
    }
}

+        err = mapstructure.WeakDecode(m, &conf)
+        if err != nil {
+                return
+        }
+
+        return
 }

+        conf = defaultConfig
+
+        if v == nil {
+                return
+        }
+
+        m := hmaps.ToStringMap(v)
+
+        // Handle deprecations.
+        if td, found := m["tdewolff"]; found {
+                tdm := hmaps.ToStringMap(td)
+
+                // Decimals was renamed to Precision in tdewolff/minify v2.7.0.
+                // https://github.com/tdewolff/minify/commit/2fed4401348ce36bd6c20e77335a463e69d94386
+                for _, key := range []string{"css", "svg"} {
+                        if v, found := tdm[key]; found {
+                                vm := hmaps.ToStringMap(v)
+                                ko := "decimals"
+                                kn := "precision"
+                                if vv, found := vm[ko]; found {
+                                        hugo.Deprecate(
+                                                fmt.Sprintf("project config key minify.tdewolff.%s.%s", key, ko),
+                                                fmt.Sprintf("Use config key minify.tdewolff.%s.%s instead.", key, kn),
+                                                "v0.150.0",
+                                        )
+                                        if _, found = vm[kn]; !found {
+                                                vvi := cast.ToInt(vv)
+                                                if vvi > 0 {
+                                                        vm[kn] = vvi
+                                                }
+                                        }
+                                        delete(vm, ko)
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+
+                // KeepConditionalComments was renamed to KeepSpecialComments in tdewolff/minify v2.20.13.
+                // https://github.com/tdewolff/minify/commit/342cbc1974162db0ad3327f7a42a623b2cd3ebbc
+                if v, found := tdm["html"]; found {
+                        vm := hmaps.ToStringMap(v)
+                        ko := "keepconditionalcomments"
+                        kn := "keepspecialcomments"
+                        if vv, found := vm[ko]; found {
+                                hugo.Deprecate(
+                                        fmt.Sprintf("project config key minify.tdewolff.html.%s", ko),
+                                        fmt.Sprintf("Use config key minify.tdewolff.html.%s instead.", kn),
+                                        "v0.150.0",
+                                )
+                                if _, found := vm[kn]; !found {
+                                        vm[kn] = cast.ToBool(vv)
+                                }
+                                delete(vm, ko)
+                        }
+                }
+
+                // KeepCSS2 was deprecated in favor of Version in tdewolff/minify v2.24.1.
+                // https://github.com/tdewolff/minify/commit/57e3ebe0e6914b82c9ab0849a14f86bc29cd2ebf
+                if v, found := tdm["css"]; found {
+                        vm := hmaps.ToStringMap(v)
+                        ko := "keepcss2"
+                        kn := "version"
+                        if vv, found := vm[ko]; found {
+                                hugo.Deprecate(
+                                        fmt.Sprintf("project config key minify.tdewolff.css.%s", ko),
+                                        fmt.Sprintf("Use config key minify.tdewolff.css.%s instead.", kn),
+                                        "v0.150.0",
+                                )
+                                if _, found := vm[kn]; !found {
+                                        if cast.ToBool(vv) {
+                                                vm[kn] = 2
+                                        }
+                                }
+                                delete(vm, ko)
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        err = mapstructure.WeakDecode(m, &conf)
+        if err != nil {
+                return
+        }
+
+        return
